<h2><span id=".E5.8F.83.E8.80.83"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="参考">参考</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%98%BF%E5%A5%91%E7%BE%8E%E5%B0%BC%E5%BE%B7%E5%B8%9D%E5%9B%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="编辑章节：参考">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id=".E5.8F.83.E8.80.83.E6.96.87.E7.8D.BB"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="参考文献">参考文献</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%98%BF%E5%A5%91%E7%BE%8E%E5%B0%BC%E5%BE%B7%E5%B8%9D%E5%9B%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="编辑章节：参考文献">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="reflist columns references-column-count references-column-count-2" style="-moz-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2; column-count: 2; list-style-type: decimal;">
<ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-EY-1"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-EY_1-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ehsan_Yarshater" title="Ehsan Yarshater">Yarshater, Ehsan</a>. The Cambridge History of Iran, Volume 3. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cambridge_University_Press" title="Cambridge University Press">Cambridge University Press</a>. 1993: 482. <a href="/wiki/Special:%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E4%B9%A6%E6%BA%90/978-0-521-20092-9" title="Special:网络书源/978-0-521-20092-9"><span title="国际标准书号">ISBN</span> 978-0-521-20092-9</a>. <q>Of the four residences of the Achaemenids named by <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Herodotus&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Herodotus（页面不存在）">Herodotus</a> — <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Ecbatana&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Ecbatana（页面不存在）">Ecbatana</a>, <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Pasargadae&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Pasargadae（页面不存在）">Pasargadae</a> or <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Persepolis" title="Persepolis">Persepolis</a>, <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Susa&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Susa（页面不存在）">Susa</a> and <a href="/wiki/Babylon" title="Babylon">Babylon</a> — the last [situated in Iraq] was maintained as their most important capital, the fixed winter quarters, the central office of bureaucracy, exchanged only in the heat of summer for some cool spot in the highlands. Under the <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Seleucid_Empire&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Seleucid Empire（页面不存在）">Seleucids</a> and the <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Parthian_Empire&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Parthian Empire（页面不存在）">Parthians</a> the site of the Mesopotamian capital moved a little to the north on the <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Tigris&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Tigris（页面不存在）">Tigris</a> — to <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Seleucia&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Seleucia（页面不存在）">Seleucia</a> and <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Ctesiphon&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Ctesiphon（页面不存在）">Ctesiphon</a>. It is indeed symbolic that these new foundations were built from the bricks of ancient <a href="/wiki/Babylon" title="Babylon">Babylon</a>, just as later <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Baghdad&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Baghdad（页面不存在）">Baghdad</a>, a little further upstream, was built out of the ruins of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sassanid_Empire" title="Sassanid Empire">Sassanian</a> double city of <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Al-Mada%27in&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Al-Mada'in（页面不存在）">Seleucia-Ctesiphon</a>.</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E9%98%BF%E5%A5%91%E7%BE%8E%E5%B0%BC%E5%BE%B7%E5%B8%9D%E5%9B%BD&amp;rft.aufirst=Ehsan&amp;rft.aulast=Yarshater&amp;rft.btitle=The+Cambridge+History+of+Iran%2C+Volume+3&amp;rft.date=1993&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.isbn=978-0-521-20092-9&amp;rft.pages=482&amp;rft.pub=Cambridge+University+Press&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>
</li>

<li id="cite_note-155"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-155">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation web"><a class="external text" href="http://www.1902encyclopedia.com/D/DAR/darius-i-the-great.html" rel="nofollow">Darius I (Darius the Great), King of Persia (from 521 BC)</a>. 1902encyclopedia.com.  <span class="reference-accessdate"> [<span class="nowrap">7 January</span> 2011]</span>. （原始内容<a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20130303132047/http://www.1902encyclopedia.com/D/DAR/darius-i-the-great.html" rel="nofollow">存档</a>于2013-03-03）.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E9%98%BF%E5%A5%91%E7%BE%8E%E5%B0%BC%E5%BE%B7%E5%B8%9D%E5%9B%BD&amp;rft.btitle=Darius+I+%28Darius+the+Great%29%2C+King+of+Persia+%28from+521+BC%29&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.pub=1902encyclopedia.com&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.1902encyclopedia.com%2FD%2FDAR%2Fdarius-i-the-great.html&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>

<li id="cite_note-156"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-156">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The words are actually inscribed on the <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Frieze&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Frieze（页面不存在）">frieze</a> of the <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=James_A._Farley_Post_Office_Building&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="James A. Farley Post Office Building（页面不存在）">James A. Farley Post Office Building</a> in the borough of Manhattan in New York City, New York.
